**Journey time** is 6:58:00.

Places to visit are m heigh tower, built between 1573 and 1576, by Heinrich Seeling in neo-Baroque style, by the Reussians, km (6 mi), established in 17th and 18th century for storing beer, in Baroque style with a surrounding park, and partial demolished in 1962, and 1720 by David Schatz in Baroque style, and 1611 as cemetery church, and 1885 in neo-Gothic style, in modern style as one of only few bigger new churches in Thuringia after 1990, in neo-Gothic style, by the famous architect Henry van de Velde.

## [Erlangen](https://en.wikivoyage.org/?curid=11066)

**Journey time** is 9:02:00.

Places to visit are Margravial Palace and the square 2 Bohlenplatz, and was rebuilt from scratch, Palais Stutterheim, Marktplatz 1, Margrave Palace (Markgräfliche Schloss), Schlossplatz, Orangerie Erlangen, Historic water tower on Apfelstraße, Apfelstraße 12, Historic water tower on the Burgberg hill, Burgbergstraße 90, Bierkeller (beer cellars) at Entlas Keller, An den Kellern 5-7 (towards the end of the "Berch" area (when entering, go left, Entlas Keller has a concrete-glass structure added which is quite obvious)), ☏ +49 9131 22100, Hugenot church, Bahnhofplatz 3 (located between the squares “Bahnhofsplatz” und “Hugenottenplatz”), Altstädter Dreifaltigkeitskirche, Martin-Luther-Platz 1, St. Martinskirche, Altstädter Friedhof 1 (within the old town cemetery on Martinsbühl)., University Church of the New Town (Neustädter Kirche), Neustädter Kirchplatz 1, German reformed church Bohlenplatz, Bohlenplatz 1, Herz-Jesu-Kirche, Kunstpalais, Palais Sutterheim, Marktplatz 1 (south-western end of the central market square (Marktplatz/Schlossplatz, with Hauptstraße passing trough)), ☏ +49 9131 86-2735, info@kunstpalais, Kunstmuseum Erlangen, Loewenichsches Palais, Nürnberger Straße 9 (in front of the northern entrance of the Erlangen arcaden, at the intersection of Nürnberger Straße and Henkestraße), ☏ +49 9131 2041555, kunstmuseum@stadt, Kunstverein Erlangen,
